So I\r","intend to prove the kitten's innocence by a trick.\"\r","\r","He drew from his inside pocket one of the eight tiny piglets that were\r","remaining and continued:\r","\r","\"This creature you must hide in some safe place, and if the jury decides\r","that Eureka is guilty you may then produce this piglet and claim it is\r","the one that was lost. All the piglets are exactly alike, so no one can\r","dispute your word. This deception will save Eureka's life, and then we\r","may all be happy again.\"\r","\r","\"I do not like to deceive my friends,\" replied the Tin Woodman; \"still,\r","my kind heart urges me to save Eureka's life, and I can usually trust my\r","heart to do the right thing. So I will do as you say, friend Wizard.\"\r","\r","After some thought he placed the little pig inside his funnel-shaped\r","hat, and then put the hat upon his head and went back to his room to\r","think over his speech to the jury.\r","\r","\r","\r","\r","CHAPTER 19.\r","\r","THE WIZARD PERFORMS ANOTHER TRICK\r","\r","\r","At three o'clock the Throne Room was crowded with citizens, men, women\r","and children being eager to witness the great trial.\r","\r","Princess Ozma, dressed in her most splendid robes of state, sat in the\r","magnificent emerald throne, with her jewelled sceptre in her hand and\r","her sparkling coronet upon her fair brow. Behind her throne stood the\r","twenty-eight officers of her army and many officials of the royal\r","household. At her right sat the queerly assorted Jury--animals, animated\r","dummies and people--all gravely prepared to listen to what was said. The\r","kitten had been placed in a large cage just before the throne, where she\r","sat upon her haunches and gazed through the bars at the crowds around\r","her, with seeming unconcern.\r","\r","And now, at a signal from Ozma, the Woggle-Bug arose and addressed the\r","jury. His tone was pompous and he strutted up and down in an absurd\r","attempt to appear dignified.\r","\r","\"Your Royal Highness and Fellow Citizens,\" he began; \"the small cat you\r","see a prisoner before you is accused of the crime of first murdering and\r","then eating our esteemed Ruler's fat piglet--or else first eating and\r","then murdering it. In either case a grave crime has been committed which\r","deserves a grave punishment.\"\r","\r","\"Do you mean my kitten must be put in a grave?\" asked Dorothy.\r","\r","\"Don't interrupt, little girl,\" said the Woggle-Bug. \"When I get my\r","thoughts arranged in good order I do not like to have anything upset\r","them or throw them into confusion.\"\r","\r","\"If your thoughts were any good they wouldn't become confused,\" remarked\r","the Scarecrow, earnestly. \"My thoughts are always----\"\r","\r","\"Is this a trial of thoughts, or of kittens?\" demanded the Woggle-Bug.\r","\r","\"It's a trial of one kitten,\" replied the Scarecrow; \"but your manner is\r","a trial to us all.\"\r","\r","\"Let the Public Accuser continue,\" called Ozma from her throne, \"and I\r","pray you do not interrupt him.\"\r","\r","\"The criminal who now sits before the court licking her paws,\" resumed\r","the Woggle-Bug, \"has long desired to unlawfully eat the fat piglet,\r","which was no bigger than a mouse. And finally she made a wicked plan to\r","satisfy her depraved appetite for pork. I can see her, in my mind's\r","eye----\"\r","\r","\"What's that?\" asked the Scarecrow.\r","\r","\"I say I can see her in my mind's eye----\"\r","\r","\"The mind has no eye,\" declared the Scarecrow. \"It's blind.\"\r","\r","\"Your Highness,\" cried the Woggle-Bug, appealing to Ozma, \"have I a\r","mind's eye, or haven't I?\"\r","\r","\"If you have, it is invisible,\" said the Princess.\r","\r","\"Very true,\" returned the Woggle-Bug, bowing. \"I say I see the criminal,\r","in my mind's eye, creeping stealthily into the room of our Ozma and\r","secreting herself, when no one was looking, until the Princess had gone\r","away and the door was closed. Then the murderer was alone with her\r","helpless victim, the fat piglet, and I see her pounce upon the innocent\r","creature and eat it up----\"\r","\r","\"Are you still seeing with your mind's eye?\" enquired the Scarecrow.\r","\r","\"Of course; how else could I see it? And we know the thing is true,\r","because since the time of that interview there is no piglet to be found\r","anywhere.\"\r","\r","[Illustration: EUREKA IN COURT.]\r","\r","\"I suppose, if the cat had been gone, instead of the piglet, your mind's\r","eye would see the piglet eating the cat,\" suggested the Scarecrow.\r","\r","\"Very likely,\" acknowledged the Woggle-Bug. \"And now, Fellow Citizens\r","and Creatures of the Jury, I assert that so awful a crime deserves\r","death, and in the case of the ferocious criminal before you--who is now\r","washing her face--the death penalty should be inflicted nine times.\"\r","\r","There was great applause when the speaker sat down. Then the Princess\r","spoke in a stern voice:\r","\r","\"Prisoner, what have you to say for yourself? Are you guilty, or not\r","guilty?\"\r","\r","\"Why, that's for you to find out,\" replied Eureka. \"If you can prove I'm\r","guilty, I'll be willing to die nine times, but a mind's eye is no proof,\r","because the Woggle-Bug has no mind to see with.\"\r","\r","\"Never mind, dear,\" said Dorothy.\r","\r","Then the Tin Woodman arose and said:\r","\r","\"Respected Jury and dearly beloved Ozma, I pray you not to judge this\r","feline prisoner unfeelingly. I do not think the innocent kitten can be\r","guilty, and surely it is unkind to accuse a luncheon of being a murder.\r","Eureka is the sweet pet of a lovely little girl whom we all admire, and\r","gentleness and innocence are her chief virtues. Look at the kitten's\r","intelligent eyes;\" (here Eureka closed her eyes sleepily) \"gaze at her\r","smiling countenance!\" (here Eureka snarled and showed her teeth) \"mark\r","the tender pose of her soft, padded little hands!\" (Here Eureka bared\r","her sharp claws and scratched at the bars of the cage.) \"Would such a\r","gentle animal be guilty of eating a fellow creature? No; a thousand\r","times, no!\"\r","\r","\"Oh, cut it short,\" said Eureka; \"you've talked long enough.\"\r","\r","\"I'm trying to defend you,\" remonstrated the Tin Woodman.\r","\r","\"Then say something sensible,\" retorted the kitten. \"Tell them it would\r","be foolish for me to eat the piglet, because I had sense enough to know\r","it would raise a row if I did. But don't try to make out I'm too\r","innocent to eat a fat piglet if I could do it and not be found out. I\r","imagine it would taste mighty good.\"\r","\r","\"Perhaps it would, to those who eat,\" remarked the Tin Woodman. \"I\r","myself, not being built to eat, have no personal experience in such\r","matters. But I remember that our great poet once said:\r","\r","    \"'To eat is sweet\r","    When hunger's seat\r","    Demands a treat\r","    Of savory meat.'\r","\r","\"Take this into consideration, friends of the Jury, and you will readily\r","decide that the kitten is wrongfully accused and should be set at\r","liberty.\"\r","\r","When the Tin Woodman sat down no one applauded him, for his arguments\r","had not been very convincing and few believed that he had proved\r","Eureka's innocence. As for the Jury, the members whispered to each other\r","for a few minutes and then they appointed the Hungry Tiger their\r","spokesman. The huge beast slowly arose and said:\r","\r","\"Kittens have no consciences, so they eat whatever pleases them. The\r","jury believes the white kitten known as Eureka is guilty of having eaten\r","the piglet owned by Princess Ozma, and recommends that she be put to\r","death in punishment of the crime.\"\r","\r","The judgment of the jury was received with great applause, although\r","Dorothy was sobbing miserably at the fate of her pet. The Princess was\r","just about to order Eureka's head chopped off with the Tin Woodman's axe\r","when that brilliant personage once more arose and addressed her.\r","\r","\"Your Highness,\" said he, \"see how easy it is for a jury to be mistaken.\r","The kitten could not have eaten your piglet--for here it is!\"\r","\r","He took off his funnel hat and from beneath it produced a tiny white\r","piglet, which he held aloft that all might see it clearly.\r","\r","Ozma was delighted and exclaimed, eagerly:\r","\r","\"Give me my pet, Nick Chopper!\"\r","\r","And all the people cheered and clapped their hands, rejoicing that the\r","prisoner had escaped death and been proved to be innocent.\r","\r","As the Princess held the white piglet in her arms and stroked its soft\r","hair she said: \"Let Eureka out of the cage, for she is no longer a\r","prisoner, but our good friend. Where did you find my missing pet, Nick\r","Chopper?\"\r","\r","\"In a room of the palace,\" he answered.\r","\r","\"Justice,\" remarked the Scarecrow, with a sigh, \"is a dangerous thing to\r","meddle with. If you hadn't happened to find the piglet, Eureka would\r","surely have been executed.\"\r","\r","\"But justice prevailed at the last,\" said Ozma, \"for here is my pet, and\r","Eureka is once more free.\"\r","\r","\"I refuse to be free,\" cried the kitten, in a sharp voice, \"unless the\r","Wizard can do his trick with eight piglets. If he can produce but seven,\r","then this it not the piglet that was lost, but another one.\"\r","\r","\"Hush, Eureka!\" warned the Wizard.\r","\r","\"Don't be foolish,\" advised the Tin Woodman, \"or you may be sorry for\r","it.\"\r","\r","\"The piglet that belonged to the Princess wore an emerald collar,\" said\r","Eureka, loudly enough for all to hear.\r","\r","\"So it did!\" exclaimed Ozma. \"This cannot be the one the Wizard gave\r","me.\"\r","\r","\"Of course not; he had nine of them, altogether,\" declared Eureka; \"and\r","I must say it was very stingy of him not to let me eat just a few. But\r","now that this foolish trial is ended, I will tell you what really became\r","of your pet piglet.\"\r","\r","At this everyone in the Throne Room suddenly became quiet, and the\r","kitten continued, in a calm, mocking tone of voice:\r","\r","\"I will confess that I intended to eat the little pig for my breakfast;\r","so I crept into the room where it was kept while the Princess was\r","dressing and hid myself under a chair. When Ozma went away she closed\r","the door and left her pet on the table. At once I jumped up and told the\r","piglet not to make a fuss, for he would be inside of me in half a\r","second; but no one can teach one of these creatures to be reasonable.\r","Instead of keeping still, so I could eat him comfortably, he trembled so\r","with fear that he fell off the table into a big vase that was standing\r","on the floor. The vase had a very small neck, and spread out at the top\r","like a bowl. At first the piglet stuck in the neck of the vase and I\r","thought I should get him, after all, but he wriggled himself through and\r","fell down into the deep bottom part--and I suppose he's there yet.\"\r","\r","All were astonished at this confession, and Ozma at once sent an officer\r","to her room to fetch the vase. When he returned the Princess looked down\r","the narrow neck of the big ornament and discovered her lost piglet, just\r","as Eureka had said she would.\r","\r","There was no way to get the creature out without breaking the vase, so\r","the Tin Woodman smashed it with his axe and set the little prisoner\r","free.\r","\r","Then the crowd cheered lustily and Dorothy hugged the kitten in her arms\r","and told her how delighted she was to know that she was innocent.\r","\r","\"But why didn't you tell us at first?\" she asked.\r","\r","\"It would have spoiled the fun,\" replied the kitten, yawning.\r","\r","Ozma gave the Wizard back the piglet he had so kindly allowed Nick\r","Chopper to substitute for the lost one, and then she carried her own\r","into the apartments of the palace where she lived. And now, the trial\r","being over, the good citizens of the Emerald City scattered to their\r","homes, well content with the day's amusement.\r","\r","\r","\r","\r","CHAPTER 20.\r","\r","ZEB RETURNS TO THE RANCH\r","\r","\r","Eureka was much surprised to find herself in disgrace; but she was, in\r","spite of the fact that she had not eaten the piglet. For the folks of Oz\r","knew the kitten had tried to commit the crime, and that only an accident\r","had prevented her from doing so; therefore even the Hungry Tiger\r","preferred not to associate with her. Eureka was forbidden to wander\r","around the palace and was made to stay in confinement in Dorothy's room;\r","so she began to beg her mistress to send her to some other place where\r","she could enjoy herself better.\r","\r","Dorothy was herself anxious to get home, so she promised Eureka they\r","would not stay in the Land of Oz much longer.\r","\r","The next evening after the trial the little girl begged Ozma to allow\r","her to look in the enchanted picture, and the Princess readily\r","consented. She took the child to her room and said: \"Make your wish,\r","dear, and the picture will show the scene you desire to behold.\"\r","\r","Then Dorothy found, with the aid of the enchanted picture, that Uncle\r","Henry had returned to the farm in Kansas, and she also saw that both he\r","and Aunt Em were dressed in mourning, because they thought their little\r","niece had been killed by the earthquake.\r","\r","\"Really,\" said the girl, anxiously, \"I must get back as soon as poss'ble\r","to my own folks.\"\r","\r","Zeb also wanted to see his home, and although he did not find anyone\r","mourning for him, the sight of Hugson's Ranch in the picture made him\r","long to get back there.\r","\r","\"This is a fine country, and I like all the people that live in it,\" he\r","told Dorothy. \"But the fact is, Jim and I don't seem to fit into a\r","fairyland, and the old horse has been begging me to go home again ever\r","since he lost the race. So, if you can find a way to fix it, we'll be\r","much obliged to you.\"\r","\r","\"Ozma can do it, easily,\" replied Dorothy. \"Tomorrow morning I'll go to\r","Kansas and you can go to Californy.\"\r","\r","[Illustration: \"I'M MUCH OBLIGED FOR ALL YOUR KINDNESS.\"]\r","\r","That last evening was so delightful that the boy will never forget it as\r","long as he lives. They were all together (except Eureka) in the\r","pretty rooms of the Princess, and the Wizard did some new tricks, and\r","the Scarecrow told stories, and the Tin Woodman sang a love song in a\r","sonorous, metallic voice, and everybody laughed and had a good time.\r","Then Dorothy wound up Tik-tok and he danced a jig to amuse the company,\r","after which the Yellow Hen related some of her adventures with the Nome\r","King in the Land of Ev.\r","\r","The Princess served delicious refreshments to those who were in the\r","habit of eating, and when Dorothy's bed time arrived the company\r","separated after exchanging many friendly sentiments.\r","\r","Next morning they all assembled for the final parting, and many of the\r","officials and courtiers came to look upon the impressive ceremonies.\r","\r","Dorothy held Eureka in her arms and bade her friends a fond good-bye.\r","\r","\"You must come again, some time,\" said the little Wizard; and she\r","promised she would if she found it possible to do so.\r","\r","\"But Uncle Henry and Aunt Em need me to help them,\" she added, \"so I\r","can't ever be very long away from the farm in Kansas.\"\r","\r","Ozma wore the Magic Belt; and, when she had kissed Dorothy farewell and\r","had made her wish, the little girl and her kitten disappeared in a\r","twinkling.\r","\r","\"Where is she?\" asked Zeb, rather bewildered by the suddenness of it.\r","\r","\"Greeting her uncle and aunt in Kansas, by this time,\" returned Ozma,\r","with a smile.\r","\r","Then Zeb brought out Jim, all harnessed to the buggy, and took his seat.\r","\r","\"I'm much obliged for all your kindness,\" said the boy, \"and very\r","grateful to you for saving my life and sending me home again after all\r","the good times I've had. I think this is the loveliest country in the\r","world; but not being fairies Jim and I feel we ought to be where we\r","belong--and that's at the ranch. Good-bye, everybody!\"\r","\r","He gave a start and rubbed his eyes. Jim was trotting along the\r","well-known road, shaking his ears and whisking his tail with a contented\r","motion. Just ahead of them were the gates of Hugson's Ranch, and Uncle\r","Hugson now came out and stood with uplifted arms and wide open mouth,\r","staring in amazement.\r","\r","\"Goodness gracious! It's Zeb--and Jim, too!\" he exclaimed. \"Where in the\r","world have you been, my lad?\"\r","\r","\"Why, in the world, Uncle,\" answered Zeb, with a laugh.\r","\r","The </div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC22" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="22" style="position:relative">         *       *       *       *       *</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC23" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="23" style="position:relative">

</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC28" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="28" style="position:relative">  DEDICATED TO HARRIET A. B. NEAL.</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC29" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="29" style="position:relative">
</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC30" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="30" style="position:relative">
</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC31" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="31" style="position:relative">         *       *       *       *       *</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC32" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="32" style="position:relative">
</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC33" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="33" style="position:relative">
</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC34" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="34" style="position:relative">To My Readers</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC35" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="35" style="position:relative">
</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC36" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="36" style="position:relative">
</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC37" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="37" style="position:relative">It&#039;s no use; no use at all. The children won&#039;t let me stop telling tales</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC38" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="38" style="position:relative">of the Land of Oz. I know lots of other stories, and I hope to tell</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC39" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="39" style="position:relative">them, some time or another; but just now my loving tyrants won&#039;t allow</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC40" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="40" style="position:relative">me. They cry: &quot;Oz--Oz! more about Oz, Mr. Baum!&quot; and what can I do but</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC41" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="41" style="position:relative">obey their commands?</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC42" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="42" style="position:relative">
</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC43" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="43" style="position:relative">This is Our Book--mine and the children&#039;s. For they have flooded me with</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC44" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="44" style="position:relative">thousands of suggestions in regard to it, and I have honestly tried to</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC45" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="45" style="position:relative">adopt as many of these suggestions as could be fitted into one story.</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC46" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="46" style="position:relative">
</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC47" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="47" style="position:relative">After the wonderful success of &quot;Ozma of Oz&quot; it is evident that Dorothy</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC48" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="48" style="position:relative">has become a firm fixture in these Oz stories. The little ones all love</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC49" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="49" style="position:relative">Dorothy, and as one of my small friends aptly states: &quot;It isn&#039;t a real</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC50" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="50" style="position:relative">Oz story without her.&quot; So here she is again, as sweet and gentle and</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC51" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="51" style="position:relative">innocent as ever, I hope, and the heroine of another strange adventure.</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC52" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="52" style="position:relative">
</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC53" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="53" style="position:relative">There were many requests from my little correspondents for &quot;more about</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC54" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="54" style="position:relative">the Wizard.&quot; It seems the jolly old fellow made hosts of friends in the</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC55" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="55" style="position:relative">first Oz book, in spite of the fact that he frankly acknowledged himself</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC56" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="56" style="position:relative">&quot;a humbug.&quot; The children had heard how he mounted into the sky in a</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC57" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="57" style="position:relative">balloon and they were all waiting for him to come down again. So what</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC58" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="58" style="position:relative">could I do but tell &quot;what happened to the Wizard afterward&quot;? You will</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC59" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="59" style="position:relative">find him in these pages, just the same humbug Wizard as before.</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC60" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="60" style="position:relative">
</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC61" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="61" style="position:relative">There was one thing the children demanded which I found it impossible to</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC62" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="62" style="position:relative">do in this present book: they bade me introduce Toto, Dorothy&#039;s little</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC63" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="63" style="position:relative">black dog, who has many friends among my readers. But you will see, when</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC64" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="64" style="position:relative">you begin to read the story, that Toto was in Kansas while Dorothy was</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC65" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="65" style="position:relative">in California, and so she had to start on her adventure without him. In</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC66" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="66" style="position:relative">this book Dorothy had to take her kitten with her instead of her dog;</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC67" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="67" style="position:relative">but in the next Oz book, if I am permitted to write one, I intend to</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC68" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="68" style="position:relative">tell a good deal about Toto&#039;s further history.</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC69" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="69" style="position:relative">
</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC70" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="70" style="position:relative">Princess Ozma, whom I love as much as my readers do, is again introduced</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC71" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="71" style="position:relative">in this story, and so are several of our old friends of Oz. You will</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC72" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="72" style="position:relative">also become acquainted with Jim the Cab-Horse, the Nine Tiny Piglets,</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC73" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="73" style="position:relative">and Eureka, the Kitten. I am sorry the kitten was not as well behaved as</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC74" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="74" style="position:relative">she ought to have been; but perhaps she wasn&#039;t brought up properly.</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC75" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="75" style="position:relative">Dorothy found her, you see, and who her parents were nobody knows.</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC76" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="76" style="position:relative">
</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC77" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="77" style="position:relative">I believe, my dears, that I am the proudest story-teller that ever</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC78" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="78" style="position:relative">lived. Many a time tears of pride and joy have stood in my eyes while I</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC79" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="79" style="position:relative">read the tender, loving, appealing letters that come to me in almost</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC80" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="80" style="position:relative">every mail from my little readers. To have pleased you, to have</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC81" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="81" style="position:relative">interested you, to have won your friendship, and perhaps your love,</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC82" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="82" style="position:relative">through my stories, is to my mind as great an achievement as to become</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC83" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="83" style="position:relative">President of the United States. Indeed, I would much rather be your</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC84" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="84" style="position:relative">story-teller, under these conditions, than to be the President. So you</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC85" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="85" style="position:relative">have helped me to fulfill my life&#039;s ambition, and I am more grateful to</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC86" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="86" style="position:relative">you, my dears, than I can express in words.</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC87" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="87" style="position:relative">
</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC88" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="88" style="position:relative">I try to answer every letter of my young correspondents; yet sometimes</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC89" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="89" style="position:relative">there are so many letters that a little time must pass before you get</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC90" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="90" style="position:relative">your answer. But be patient, friends, for the answer will surely come,</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC91" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="91" style="position:relative">and by writing to me you more than repay me for the pleasant task of</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC92" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="92" style="position:relative">preparing these books. Besides, I am proud to acknowledge that the books</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC93" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="93" style="position:relative">are partly yours, for your suggestions often guide me in telling the</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC94" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="94" style="position:relative">stories, and I am sure they would not be half so good without your</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC95" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="95" style="position:relative">clever and thoughtful assistance.</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC96" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="96" style="position:relative">
</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC97" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="97" style="position:relative">                                                     L. </div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC282" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="282" style="position:relative">&quot;What is your name?&quot; asked Dorothy, thinking she liked the boy&#039;s manner</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC283" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="283" style="position:relative">and the cheery tone of his voice.</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC284" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="284" style="position:relative">
</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC285" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="285" style="position:relative">&quot;Not a very pretty one,&quot; he answered, as if a little ashamed. &quot;My whole</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC286" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="286" style="position:relative">name is Zebediah; but folks just call me &#039;Zeb.&#039; You&#039;ve been to</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC287" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="287" style="position:relative">Australia, haven&#039;t you?&quot;</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC288" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="288" style="position:relative">
</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC289" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="289" style="position:relative">&quot;Yes; with Uncle Henry,&quot; she answered. &quot;We got to San Francisco a week</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC290" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="290" style="position:relative">ago, and Uncle Henry went right on to Hugson&#039;s Ranch for a visit while I</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC291" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="291" style="position:relative">stayed a few days in the city with some friends we had met.&quot;</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC292" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="292" style="position:relative">
</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC293" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="293" style="position:relative">&quot;How long will you be with us?&quot; he asked.</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC294" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="294" style="position:relative">
</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC295" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="295" style="position:relative">&quot;Only a day. Tomorrow Uncle Henry and I must start back for Kansas.</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC296" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="296" style="position:relative">We&#039;ve been away for a long time, you know, and so we&#039;re anxious to get</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC297" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="297" style="position:relative">home again.&quot;</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC298" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="298" style="position:relative">
</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC299" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="299" style="position:relative">The boy flicked the big, boney horse with his whip and looked</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC300" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="300" style="position:relative">thoughtful. Then he started to say something to his little companion,</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC301" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="301" style="position:relative">but before he could speak the buggy began to sway dangerously from side</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC302" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="302" style="position:relative">to side and the earth seemed to rise up before them. Next minute there</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC303" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="303" style="position:relative">was a roar and a sharp crash, and at her side Dorothy saw the ground</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC304" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="304" style="position:relative">open in a wide crack and then come together again.</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC305" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="305" style="position:relative">
</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC306" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="306" style="position:relative">&quot;Goodness!&quot; she cried, grasping the iron rail of the seat. &quot;What was</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC307" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="307" style="position:relative">that?&quot;</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC308" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="308" style="position:relative">
</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC309" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="309" style="position:relative">&quot;That was an awful big quake,&quot; replied Zeb, with a white face. &quot;It</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC310" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="310" style="position:relative">almost got us that time, Dorothy.&quot;</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC311" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="311" style="position:relative">
</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC312" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="312" style="position:relative">The horse had stopped short, and stood firm as a rock. Zeb shook the</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC313" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="313" style="position:relative">reins and urged him to go, but Jim was stubborn. Then the boy cracked</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC314" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="314" style="position:relative">his whip and touched the animal&#039;s flanks with it, and after a low moan</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC315" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="315" style="position:relative">of protest Jim stepped slowly along the road.</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC316" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="316" style="position:relative">
</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC317" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="317" style="position:relative">Neither the boy nor the girl spoke again for some minutes. There was a</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC318" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="318" style="position:relative">breath of danger in the very air, and every few moments the earth would</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC319" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="319" style="position:relative">shake violently. Jim&#039;s ears were standing erect upon his head and every</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC320" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="320" style="position:relative">muscle of his big body was tense as he trotted toward home. He was not</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC321" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="321" style="position:relative">going very fast, but on his flanks specks of foam began to appear and at</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC322" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="322" style="position:relative">times he would tremble like a leaf.</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC323" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="323" style="position:relative">
</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC324" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="324" style="position:relative">The sky had grown darker again and the wind made queer sobbing sounds as</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC325" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="325" style="position:relative">it swept over the valley.</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC326" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="326" style="position:relative">
</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC327" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="327" style="position:relative">Suddenly there was a rending, tearing sound, and the earth split into</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC328" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="328" style="position:relative">another great crack just beneath the spot where the horse was standing.</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC329" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="329" style="position:relative">With a wild neigh of terror the animal fell bodily into the pit, drawing</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC330" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="330" style="position:relative">the buggy and its occupants after him.</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC331" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="331" style="position:relative">
</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC332" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="332" style="position:relative">Dorothy grabbed fast hold of the buggy top and the boy did the same. The</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC333" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="333" style="position:relative">sudden rush into space confused them so that they could not think.</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC334" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="334" style="position:relative">
</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC335" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="335" style="position:relative">Blackness engulfed them on every side, and in breathless silence they</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC336" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="336" style="position:relative">waited for the fall to end and crush them against jagged rocks or for</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC337" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="337" style="position:relative">the earth to close in on them again and bury them forever in its</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC338" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="338" style="position:relative">dreadful depths.</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC339" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="339" style="position:relative">
</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC340" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="340" style="position:relative">The horrible sensation of falling, the darkness and the terrifying</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC341" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="341" style="position:relative">noises, proved more than Dorothy could endure and for a few moments the</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC342" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="342" style="position:relative">little girl lost consciousness. Zeb, being a boy, did not faint, but he</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC343" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="343" style="position:relative">was badly frightened, and clung to the buggy seat with a tight grip,</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC344" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="344" style="position:relative">expecting every moment would be his last.</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC345" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="345" style="position:relative">
</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC346" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="346" style="position:relative">[Illustration]</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC347" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="347" style="position:relative">
</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC348" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="348" style="position:relative">[Illustration]</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC349" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="349" style="position:relative">
</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC350" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="350" style="position:relative">
</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC351" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="351" style="position:relative">
</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC352" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="352" style="position:relative">
</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC353" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="353" style="position:relative">CHAPTER 2.</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC354" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="354" style="position:relative">
</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC355" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="355" style="position:relative">THE GLASS CITY</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC356" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="356" style="position:relative">
</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC357" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="357" style="position:relative">
</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC358" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="358" style="position:relative">When Dorothy recovered her senses they were still falling, but not so</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC359" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="359" style="position:relative">fast. The top of the buggy caught the air like a parachute or an</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC360" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="360" style="position:relative">umbrella filled with wind, and held them back so that they floated</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC361" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="361" style="position:relative">downward with a gentle motion that was not so very disagreeable to bear.</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC362" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="362" style="position:relative">The worst thing was their terror of reaching the bottom of this great</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC363" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="363" style="position:relative">crack in the earth, and the natural fear that sudden death was about to</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC364" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="364" style="position:relative">overtake them at any moment. Crash after crash echoed far above their</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC365" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="365" style="position:relative">heads, as the earth came together where it had split, and stones and</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC366" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="366" style="position:relative">chunks of clay rattled around them on every side. These they could not</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC367" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="367" style="position:relative">see, but they could feel them pelting the buggy top, and Jim screamed</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC368" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="368" style="position:relative">almost like a human being when a stone overtook him and struck his</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC369" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="369" style="position:relative">boney body. They did not really hurt the poor horse, because everything</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC370" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="370" style="position:relative">was falling together; only the stones and rubbish fell faster than the</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC371" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="371" style="position:relative">horse and buggy, which were held back by the pressure of the air, so</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC372" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="372" style="position:relative">that the terrified animal was actually more frightened than he was</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC373" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="373" style="position:relative">injured.</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC374" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="374" style="position:relative">
</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC375" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="375" style="position:relative">How long this state of things continued Dorothy could not even guess,</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC376" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="376" style="position:relative">she was so greatly bewildered. But bye and bye, as she stared ahead into</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC377" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="377" style="position:relative">the black chasm with a beating heart, she began to dimly see the form of</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC378" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="378" style="position:relative">the horse Jim--his head up in the air, his ears erect and his long legs</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC379" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="379" style="position:relative">sprawling in every direction as he tumbled through space. Also, turning</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC380" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="380" style="position:relative">her head, she found that she could see the boy beside her, who had until</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC381" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="381" style="position:relative">now remained as still and silent as she herself.</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC382" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="382" style="position:relative">
</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC383" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="383" style="position:relative">Dorothy sighed and commenced to breathe easier. She began to realize</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC384" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="384" style="position:relative">that death was not in store for her, after all, but that she had merely</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC385" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="385" style="position:relative">started upon another adventure, which promised to be just as queer and</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC386" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="386" style="position:relative">unusual as were those she had before encountered.</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC387" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="387" style="position:relative">
</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC388" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="388" style="position:relative">With this thought in mind the girl took heart and leaned her head over</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC389" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="389" style="position:relative">the side of the buggy to see where the strange light was coming from.</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC390" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="390" style="position:relative">Far below her she found six great glowing balls suspended in the air.</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC391" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="391" style="position:relative">The central and largest one was white, and reminded her of the sun.</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC392" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="392" style="position:relative">Around it were arranged, like the five points of a star, the other five</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC393" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="393" style="position:relative">brilliant balls; one being rose colored, one violet, one yellow, one</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC394" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="394" style="position:relative">blue and one orange. This splendid group of colored suns sent rays</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC395" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="395" style="position:relative">darting in every direction, and as the horse and buggy--with Dorothy and</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC396" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="396" style="position:relative">Zeb--sank steadily downward and came nearer to the lights, the rays</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC397" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="397" style="position:relative">began to take on all the delicate tintings of a rainbow, growing more</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC398" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="398" style="position:relative">and more distinct every moment until all the space was brilliantly</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC399" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="399" style="position:relative">illuminated.</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC400" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="400" style="position:relative">
</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC401" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="401" style="position:relative">Dorothy was too dazed to say much, but she watched one of Jim&#039;s big ears</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC402" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="402" style="position:relative">turn to violet and the other to rose, and wondered that his tail should</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC403" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="403" style="position:relative">be yellow and his body striped with blue and orange like the stripes of</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC404" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="404" style="position:relative">a zebra. Then she looked at Zeb, whose face was blue and whose hair was</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC405" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="405" style="position:relative">pink, and gave a little laugh that sounded a bit nervous.</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC406" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="406" style="position:relative">
</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC407" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="407" style="position:relative">&quot;Isn&#039;t it funny?&quot; she said.</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC408" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="408" style="position:relative">
</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC409" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="409" style="position:relative">The boy was startled and his eyes were big. </div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC413" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="413" style="position:relative">&quot;I--I don&#039;t s-s-see any-thing funny--&#039;bout it!&quot; he stammered.</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC414" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="414" style="position:relative">
</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC415" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="415" style="position:relative">[Illustration: HORSE, BUGGY AND ALL FELL SLOWLY.]</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC416" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="416" style="position:relative">
</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC417" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="417" style="position:relative">Just then the buggy tipped slowly over upon its side, the body of the</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC418" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="418" style="position:relative">horse tipping also. But they continued to fall, all together, and the</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC419" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="419" style="position:relative">boy and girl had no difficulty in remaining upon the seat, just as they</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC420" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="420" style="position:relative">were before. During this time Jim</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC422" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="422" style="position:relative">struggled frantically, all his legs kicking the air; but on finding</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC423" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="423" style="position:relative">himself in his former position the horse said, in a relieved tone of</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC424" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="424" style="position:relative">voice:</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC425" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="425" style="position:relative">
</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC426" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="426" style="position:relative">&quot;Well, that&#039;s better!&quot;</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC427" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="427" style="position:relative">
</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC428" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="428" style="position:relative">Dorothy and Zeb looked at one another in wonder.</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC429" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="429" style="position:relative">
</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC430" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="430" style="position:relative">&quot;Can your horse talk?&quot; she asked.</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC431" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="431" style="position:relative">
</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC432" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="432" style="position:relative">&quot;Never knew him to, before,&quot; replied the boy.</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC433" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="433" style="position:relative">
</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC434" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="434" style="position:relative">&quot;Those were the first words I ever said,&quot; called out the horse, who had</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC435" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="435" style="position:relative">overheard them, &quot;and I can&#039;t explain why I happened to speak then.
